currency_value_evolution_list = {
    every_country = {
        limit = {
            #has_modifier = has_financial_center
			has_central_bank_SS_BS_GS_GES_NISO = yes
			market_owner_is_root_univ_with_buiding = no
        }
        root = {
            add_to_variable_list = {
                name = currency_value_evolution_list
                target = prev
            }
        }
    }
    root  = {
        if = {
            clear_variable_list = list_before_order
            every_in_list = {
                variable = currency_value_evolution_list
                root = {
                    add_to_variable_list = {
                        name = list_before_order
                        target = prev
                    }
                }
            }
            clear_variable_list = currency_value_evolution_list_ordered_1
            if = {
                ordered_in_list = {
                    variable = list_before_order
                    order_by = money_value_dif_1_final
                    max = 15
                    check_range_bounds = no
                    root = {
                        add_to_variable_list = {
                            name = currency_value_evolution_list_ordered_1
                            target = prev
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        clear_variable_list = currency_value_evolution_list
    }
}
independent_economies_list = {
    every_country = {
        limit = {
			has_central_bank_SS_BS_GS_GES_NISO = yes
			market_owner_is_root_univ_with_buiding = no
			is_revolutionary = no
        }
        root = {
            add_to_variable_list = {
                name = independent_economies_list
                target = prev
            }
        }
    }
    root  = {
        if = {
            clear_variable_list = list_before_order
            every_in_list = {
                variable = independent_economies_list
                root = {
                    add_to_variable_list = {
                        name = list_before_order
                        target = prev
                    }
                }
            }
            clear_variable_list = independent_economies_list_ordered_1
            if = {
                ordered_in_list = {
                    variable = list_before_order
                    order_by = money_value_rapported_inflation
                    max = 100
                    check_range_bounds = no
                    root = {
                        add_to_variable_list = {
                            name = independent_economies_list_ordered_1
                            target = prev
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        clear_variable_list = independent_economies_list
    }
}

national_capacity_variable_list = {
    every_country = {
        limit = {
            has_modifier = has_central_bank
			market_owner_is_root_univ_with_buiding = no
        }
        root = {
            add_to_variable_list = {
                name = national_capacity_variable_list
                target = prev
            }
        }
    }
    root  = {
        if = {
            clear_variable_list = list_before_order
            every_in_list = {
                variable = national_capacity_variable_list
                root = {
                    add_to_variable_list = {
                        name = list_before_order
                        target = prev
                    }
                }
                remove_modifier = global_monetary_reference
            }
            clear_variable_list = national_capacity_variable_list_ordered_1
            ordered_in_list = {
                variable = list_before_order
                order_by = national_capacity
                min = 0
                max = 10
                check_range_bounds = no
                root = {
                    add_to_variable_list = {
                        name = national_capacity_variable_list_ordered_1
                        target = prev
                    }
                    add_to_variable_list = {
                        name = reference_currency_list_1
                        target = prev
                    }
                }
            }
            clear_variable_list = reference_currency_country_1
            ordered_in_list = {
                variable = reference_currency_list_1
                order_by = national_capacity
                min = 0
                position = 1
                max = 1
                check_range_bounds = no
                root = {
                    add_to_variable_list = {
                        name = reference_currency_country_1
                        target = prev
                    }
                }
            }
            every_in_list = {
                variable = reference_currency_country_1
                if = {
                    add_modifier = {
                        name = global_monetary_reference
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }
}
is_subject_list = {
    every_country = {
        limit = {

        root = {

                name = is_subject_list

exports_imports_variable_list = {
    every_country = {
        limit = {
            has_modifier = has_central_bank
			market_owner_is_root_univ_with_buiding = no
			export_value_in_currency > 0
			import_value_in_currency > 0
        }
        root = {
            add_to_variable_list = {
                name = exports_imports_variable_list
                target = prev
            }
        }
    }
    root  = {
        if = {
            clear_variable_list = list_before_order
            every_in_list = {
                variable = exports_imports_variable_list
                root = {
                    add_to_variable_list = {
                        name = list_before_order
                        target = prev
                    }
                }
            }
            clear_variable_list = exports_imports_variable_list_ordered_1
            if = {
                ordered_in_list = {

                    max = 15
                    check_range_bounds = no
                    root = {

                            name = exports_imports_variable_list_ordered_1
                            target = prev
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        clear_variable_list = exports_imports_variable_list
    }
}
central_bank_debt_variable_list = {
	#changement de princuipe ce n'azi plus la dette de la bank qui compter
	#modifier l'odre de pays acheter en premier à l'avenir avec un score ?

    every_country = {
        limit = {
			central_bank_metal_reserves_state_to_ensure_the_conversion_pourcent < 0.75
			has_central_bank_SS_BS_GS_GES_NISO = yes
			not = {
				#market_owner_is_root
				any_scope_state = {
					is_production_method_active = {
						building_type = building_bank
						production_method = pm_no_metal_consuption
					}
					not = {
						is_production_method_active = {
							building_type = building_bank
							production_method = pm_no_subject_currency_type
						}
					}
				}
			}
        }
        root = {
            add_to_variable_list = {
                name = central_bank_debt_variable_list
                target = prev
            }
        }
    }
    root = {
        if = {
            clear_variable_list = list_before_order
            every_in_list = {
                variable = central_bank_debt_variable_list
                root = {
                    add_to_variable_list = {
                        name = list_before_order
                        target = prev
                    }
                }
            }
            clear_global_variable_list = central_bank_debt_variable_list_ordered_1
			ordered_in_list = {
				variable = list_before_order
				order_by = remaining_debt
				max = 100
				check_range_bounds = no
				root = {
					add_to_global_variable_list = {
						name = central_bank_debt_variable_list_ordered_1
						target = prev
					}
				}
			}
        }
        clear_variable_list = central_bank_debt_variable_list
    }
}
country_index_variable_list = {
    every_country = {
        limit = {
            has_modifier = has_financial_center
        }
        root = {
            add_to_variable_list = {
                name = country_index_variable_list
                target = prev
            }
        }
    }
    root  = {
        if = {
            clear_variable_list = list_before_order
            every_in_list = {
                variable = country_index_variable_list
                root = {
                    add_to_variable_list = {
                        name = list_before_order
                        target = prev
                    }
                }
                remove_modifier = global_financial_power
            }
            clear_variable_list = country_index_variable_list_ordered_1
            ordered_in_list = {
                variable = list_before_order
                order_by = country_indice
                max = 10
                check_range_bounds = no
                root = {
                    add_to_variable_list = {
                        name = country_index_variable_list_ordered_1
                        target = prev
                    }
                    add_to_variable_list = {
                        name = financial_power_list_1
                        target = prev
                    }
                }
            }
            clear_variable_list = financial_power_country_1
            ordered_in_list = {
                variable = financial_power_list_1
                order_by = country_indice
                min = 0
                position = 1
                max = 1
                check_range_bounds = no
                root = {
                    add_to_variable_list = {
                        name = financial_power_country_1
                        target = prev
                    }
                }
            }
            every_in_list = {
                variable = financial_power_country_1
                if = {
                    add_modifier = {
                        name = global_financial_power
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        clear_variable_list = country_index_variable_list
    }
}

country_rating_A_list = {
    every_country = {
        limit = {
            has_modifier = has_central_bank
            has_modifier = has_financial_center
            OR = {
                has_modifier = country_credit_rating_AAA
                has_modifier = country_credit_rating_AA
                has_modifier = country_credit_rating_A
            }
        }
        root = {
            add_to_variable_list = {
                name = country_rating_A_list_1
                target = prev
            }
        }
    }
    root  = {
        if = {
            clear_variable_list = list_before_order
            every_in_list = {
                variable = country_rating_A_list_1
                root = {
                    add_to_variable_list = {
                        name = list_before_order
                        target = prev
                    }
                }
            }
            clear_variable_list = country_rating_A_list_ordered_1
            if = {
                ordered_in_list = {
                    variable = list_before_order
                    order_by = country_credit_pondered_mean
                    max = 100
                    check_range_bounds = no
                    root = {
                        add_to_variable_list = {
                            name = country_rating_A_list_ordered_1
                            target = prev
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        clear_variable_list = country_rating_A_list_1
    }
}

central_bank_debt_buyer_list_1_clear = {
	clear_variable_list = central_bank_debt_buyer_list_1
    every_country = {
		limit = {
			#var:ai_bond_quantity_1 > 0
			or = {
				var:ai_seller_country_general_1 = root
				var:seller_country_general_1 = root
			}
		}
		root = {
			add_to_variable_list = {
			    name = central_bank_debt_buyer_list_1
			    target = prev
			}
		}
	}
}

			    name = central_bank_debt_buyer_list_7
			    target = prev
			}
		}
	}
}

national_debt_variable_list = {
    every_country = {
        limit = {
            has_modifier = has_central_bank
			#global_country_ranking < 50
			national_debt > 0
            NOT = {
                is_subject = yes

                is_subject_type = subject_type_protectorate
            }
        }
        root = {
            add_to_variable_list = {
                name = national_debt_variable_list
                target = prev
            }
        }
    }
    root  = {
        if = {
            clear_variable_list = list_before_order
            every_in_list = {
                variable = national_debt_variable_list
                root = {
                    add_to_variable_list = {
                        name = list_before_order
                        target = prev
                    }
                }
            }
            clear_variable_list = national_debt_variable_list_ordered_1
            if = {
                ordered_in_list = {
                    variable = list_before_order
                    order_by = national_debt_compared_gdp
                    max = 15
                    check_range_bounds = no
                    root = {
                        add_to_variable_list = {
                            name = national_debt_variable_list_ordered_1
                            target = prev
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        clear_variable_list = national_debt_variable_list
    }
}
national_debt_variable_list_clear = {
	root  = {
		clear_variable_list = list_before_order
		every_in_list = {
			variable = central_bank_debt_buyer_list
			root = {
				add_to_variable_list = {
					name = list_before_order
					target = prev
				}
			}
		}
		clear_variable_list = central_bank_debt_buyer_list
		if = {
			ordered_in_list = {
				variable = list_before_order
				order_by = national_debt_compared_gdp
				max = 10
				check_range_bounds = no
				root = {
					add_to_variable_list = {
						name = central_bank_debt_buyer_list
						target = prev
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#begin_tag_2
#dinar
dinar_currency_law_list = {
	clear_variable_list = dinar_currency_law_list
	every_country = {
		limit = {
			has_law = law_type:law_dinar_currency
			has_central_bank_SS_BS_GS_GES_NISO = yes
			market_owner_is_root_univ_with_buiding = no
			not = {
				has_modifier = economic_instability
				var:currency_crisis = 1
				var:central_bank_bankruptcy = 1
				#infamy >= infamy_threshold:pariah
			}
		}
		remove_modifier = dinar_leading_currency_type
		root = {
			add_to_variable_list = {
				name = dinar_currency_law_list
				target = prev
			}
		}
	}
	root  = {
		if = {
			clear_variable_list = list_before_order
			every_in_list = {
				variable = dinar_currency_law_list
				root = {
					add_to_variable_list = {
						name = list_before_order
						target = prev
					}
				}
			}
			clear_global_variable_list = dinar_currency_law_list_ordered_1
			if = {
				ordered_in_list = {
					variable = list_before_order
					order_by = national_capacity
					max = 1
					check_range_bounds = no
					root = {
						add_to_global_variable_list = {
							name = dinar_currency_law_list_ordered_1
							target = prev
						}
					}
				}
			}
			every_in_global_list = {
				variable = dinar_currency_law_list_ordered_1
				remove_modifier = dinar_leading_currency_type
				add_modifier = {
					name = dinar_leading_currency_type
				}
			}
		}
		#clear_variable_list = dinar_currency_list
	}
	if = {
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_law = law_type:law_dinar_currency
				market_owner_is_root_univ_with_buiding = yes
			}
			remove_modifier = dinar_leading_currency_type
		}
	}
}

#dollar_sierra_leonean_dollar
dollar_sierra_leonean_dollar_currency_law_list = {
	clear_variable_list = dollar_sierra_leonean_dollar_currency_law_list
	every_country = {
		limit = {
			has_law = law_type:law_dollar_sierra_leonean_dollar_currency
			has_central_bank_SS_BS_GS_GES_NISO = yes
			market_owner_is_root_univ_with_buiding = no
			not = {
				has_modifier = economic_instability
				var:currency_crisis = 1
				var:central_bank_bankruptcy = 1
				#infamy >= infamy_threshold:pariah
			}
		}
		remove_modifier = dollar_sierra_leonean_dollar_leading_currency_type
		root = {
			add_to_variable_list = {
				name = dollar_sierra_leonean_dollar_currency_law_list
				target = prev
			}
		}
	}
	root  = {
		if = {
			clear_variable_list = list_before_order
			every_in_list = {
				variable = dollar_sierra_leonean_dollar_currency_law_list
				root = {
					add_to_variable_list = {
						name = list_before_order
						target = prev
					}
				}
			}
			clear_global_variable_list = dollar_sierra_leonean_dollar_currency_law_list_ordered_1
			if = {
				ordered_in_list = {
					variable = list_before_order
					order_by = national_capacity
					max = 1
					check_range_bounds = no
					root = {
						add_to_global_variable_list = {
							name = dollar_sierra_leonean_dollar_currency_law_list_ordered_1
							target = prev
						}
					}
				}
			}
			every_in_global_list = {
				variable = dollar_sierra_leonean_dollar_currency_law_list_ordered_1
				remove_modifier = dollar_sierra_leonean_dollar_leading_currency_type
				add_modifier = {
					name = dollar_sierra_leonean_dollar_leading_currency_type
				}
			}
		}
		#clear_variable_list = dollar_sierra_leonean_dollar_currency_list
	}
	if = {
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_law = law_type:law_dollar_sierra_leonean_dollar_currency
				market_owner_is_root_univ_with_buiding = yes
			}
			remove_modifier = dollar_sierra_leonean_dollar_leading_currency_type
		}
	}

eco_west_african_eco_currency_law_list = {
	clear_variable_list = eco_west_african_eco_currency_law_list
	every_country = {
		limit = {
			has_law = law_type:law_eco_west_african_eco_currency
			has_central_bank_SS_BS_GS_GES_NISO = yes
			market_owner_is_root_univ_with_buiding = no
			not = {
				has_modifier = economic_instability
				var:currency_crisis = 1
				var:central_bank_bankruptcy = 1
				#infamy >= infamy_threshold:pariah
			}
		}
		remove_modifier = eco_west_african_eco_leading_currency_type
		root = {
			add_to_variable_list = {
				name = eco_west_african_eco_currency_law_list
				target = prev
			}
		}
	}
	root  = {
		if = {
			clear_variable_list = list_before_order
			every_in_list = {
				variable = eco_west_african_eco_currency_law_list
				root = {
					add_to_variable_list = {
						name = list_before_order
						target = prev
					}
				}
			}
			clear_global_variable_list = eco_west_african_eco_currency_law_list_ordered_1
			if = {
				ordered_in_list = {
					variable = list_before_order
					order_by = national_capacity
					max = 1
					check_range_bounds = no
					root = {
						add_to_global_variable_list = {
							name = eco_west_african_eco_currency_law_list_ordered_1
							target = prev
						}
					}
				}
			}
			every_in_global_list = {
				variable = eco_west_african_eco_currency_law_list_ordered_1
				remove_modifier = eco_west_african_eco_leading_currency_type
				add_modifier = {
					name = eco_west_african_eco_leading_currency_type
				}
			}
		}
		#clear_variable_list = eco_west_african_eco_currency_list
	}
	if = {
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_law = law_type:law_eco_west_african_eco_currency
				market_owner_is_root_univ_with_buiding = yes
			}
			remove_modifier = eco_west_african_eco_leading_currency_type
		}
	}
}

		remove_modifier = gulden_south_german_gulden_leading_currency_type
		root = {
			add_to_variable_list = {
				name = gulden_south_german_gulden_currency_law_list
				target = prev
			}
		}
	}
	root  = {
		if = {
			clear_variable_list = list_before_order
			every_in_list = {
				variable = gulden_south_german_gulden_currency_law_list
				root = {
					add_to_variable_list = {
						name = list_before_order
						target = prev
					}
				}
			}
			clear_global_variable_list = gulden_south_german_gulden_currency_law_list_ordered_1
			if = {
				ordered_in_list = {
					variable = list_before_order
					order_by = national_capacity
					max = 1
					check_range_bounds = no
					root = {
						add_to_global_variable_list = {
							name = gulden_south_german_gulden_currency_law_list_ordered_1
							target = prev
						}
					}
				}
			}
			every_in_global_list = {
				variable = gulden_south_german_gulden_currency_law_list_ordered_1
				remove_modifier = gulden_south_german_gulden_leading_currency_type
				add_modifier = {
					name = gulden_south_german_gulden_leading_currency_type
				}
			}
		}
		#clear_variable_list = gulden_south_german_gulden_currency_list
	}
	if = {
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_law = law_type:law_gulden_south_german_gulden_currency
				market_owner_is_root_univ_with_buiding = yes
			}
			remove_modifier = gulden_south_german_gulden_leading_currency_type
		}
	}

				variable = lira_currency_law_list
				root = {
					add_to_variable_list = {
						name = list_before_order
						target = prev
					}
				}
			}
			clear_global_variable_list = lira_currency_law_list_ordered_1
			if = {
				ordered_in_list = {
					variable = list_before_order
					order_by = national_capacity
					max = 1
					check_range_bounds = no
					root = {
						add_to_global_variable_list = {
							name = lira_currency_law_list_ordered_1
							target = prev
						}
					}
				}
			}
			every_in_global_list = {
				variable = lira_currency_law_list_ordered_1
				remove_modifier = lira_leading_currency_type
				add_modifier = {
					name = lira_leading_currency_type
				}
			}
		}
		#clear_variable_list = lira_currency_list
	}
	if = {
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_law = law_type:law_lira_currency
				market_owner_is_root_univ_with_buiding = yes
			}
			remove_modifier = lira_leading_currency_type
		}
	}
}

#rupee_indian_rupee
rupee_indian_rupee_currency_law_list = {
	clear_variable_list = rupee_indian_rupee_currency_law_list
	every_country = {
		limit = {
			has_law = law_type:law_rupee_indian_rupee_currency
			has_central_bank_SS_BS_GS_GES_NISO = yes
			market_owner_is_root_univ_with_buiding = no
			not = {
				has_modifier = economic_instability
				var:currency_crisis = 1
				var:central_bank_bankruptcy = 1
				#infamy >= infamy_threshold:pariah
			}
		}
		remove_modifier = rupee_indian_rupee_leading_currency_type
		root = {
			add_to_variable_list = {
				name = rupee_indian_rupee_currency_law_list
				target = prev
			}
		}
	}
	root  = {
		if = {
			clear_variable_list = list_before_order
			every_in_list = {
				variable = rupee_indian_rupee_currency_law_list
				root = {
					add_to_variable_list = {
						name = list_before_order
						target = prev
					}
				}
			}
			clear_global_variable_list = rupee_indian_rupee_currency_law_list_ordered_1
			if = {
				ordered_in_list = {
					variable = list_before_order
					order_by = national_capacity
					max = 1
					check_range_bounds = no
					root = {
						add_to_global_variable_list = {
							name = rupee_indian_rupee_currency_law_list_ordered_1
							target = prev
						}
					}
				}
			}
			every_in_global_list = {
				variable = rupee_indian_rupee_currency_law_list_ordered_1
				remove_modifier = rupee_indian_rupee_leading_currency_type
				add_modifier = {
					name = rupee_indian_rupee_leading_currency_type
				}
			}
		}
		#clear_variable_list = rupee_indian_rupee_currency_list
	}
	if = {
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_law = law_type:law_rupee_indian_rupee_currency
				market_owner_is_root_univ_with_buiding = yes
			}
			remove_modifier = rupee_indian_rupee_leading_currency_type
		}
	}
}

			not = {
				has_modifier = economic_instability
				var:currency_crisis = 1

				ordered_in_list = {

							name = spe_baht_currency_law_list_ordered_1

					name = spe_baht_leading_currency_type

	if = {

					check_range_bounds = no
					root = {
						add_to_global_variable_list = {
							name = spe_uni_currency_law_list_ordered_1
							target = prev
						}
					}
				}
			}
			every_in_global_list = {
				variable = spe_uni_currency_law_list_ordered_1
				remove_modifier = spe_uni_leading_currency_type
				add_modifier = {
					name = spe_uni_leading_currency_type
				}
			}
		}
		#clear_variable_list = spe_uni_currency_list
	}
	if = {
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_law = law_type:law_spe_uni_currency
				market_owner_is_root_univ_with_buiding = yes
			}
			remove_modifier = spe_uni_leading_currency_type
		}
	}
}

#dinar
dinar_c_global_stokpile_variable_list = {
	every_country = {
		limit = {
            has_modifier = has_central_bank
			stockpiling_dinar_state > 0
		}
		root = {
			add_to_variable_list = {
				name = dinar_c_global_stokpile_variable_list_1
				target = prev
			}
		}
	}
	root  = {
		if = {
			clear_variable_list = list_before_order
			every_in_list = {
				variable = dinar_c_global_stokpile_variable_list_1
				root = {
					add_to_variable_list = {
						name = list_before_order
						target = prev
					}
				}
			}
			clear_variable_list = dinar_c_global_stokpile_variable_list_ordered_1
			if = {
				ordered_in_list = {
					variable = list_before_order
					order_by = dinar_c_total_stokpile
					max = 10
					check_range_bounds = no
					root = {
						add_to_variable_list = {
							name = dinar_c_global_stokpile_variable_list_ordered_1
							target = prev
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		clear_variable_list = money_supply_variable_list
	}
}

					max = 10

#spe_uni
spe_uni_c_global_stokpile_variable_list = {
	every_country = {
		limit = {
            has_modifier = has_central_bank
			stockpiling_spe_uni_state > 0
		}
		root = {
			add_to_variable_list = {
				name = spe_uni_c_global_stokpile_variable_list_1
				target = prev
			}
		}
	}
	root  = {
		if = {
			clear_variable_list = list_before_order
			every_in_list = {
				variable = spe_uni_c_global_stokpile_variable_list_1
				root = {
					add_to_variable_list = {
						name = list_before_order
						target = prev
					}
				}
			}
			clear_variable_list = spe_uni_c_global_stokpile_variable_list_ordered_1
			if = {
				ordered_in_list = {
					variable = list_before_order
					order_by = spe_uni_c_total_stokpile
					max = 10
					check_range_bounds = no
					root = {
						add_to_variable_list = {
							name = spe_uni_c_global_stokpile_variable_list_ordered_1
							target = prev
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
